Content Security Policy Configuration

Description
Content Security Policy (CSP) is an added layer of security that helps to detect and mitigate certain types of attacks, including Cross Site Scripting (XSS) and data injection attacks.

Vulnerability found in /

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
CSP is not set for URL: http://127.0.0.1:8000/
                                    GET / HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/"
['WSTG-CONF-12', 'OSHP-Content-Security-Policy']
Solutions
Configuring Content Security Policy involves adding the Content-Security-Policy HTTP header to a web page and giving it values to control what resources the user agent is allowed to load for that page.
References
  • Mozilla: Content Security Policy (CSP)
  • OWASP: Content Security Policy Cheat Sheet
  • OWASP: How to do Content Security Policy (PDF)
  • OWASP: Content Security Policy

Clickjacking Protection

Description
Clickjacking is a technique that tricks a user into clicking something different from what the user perceives, potentially revealing confidential information or taking control of their computer.

Vulnerability found in /

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
X-Frame-Options is not set
                                    GET / HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/"
['OSHP-X-Frame-Options']
Solutions
Implement X-Frame-Options or Content Security Policy (CSP) frame-ancestors directive.
References
  • OWASP: Clickjacking
  • KeyCDN: Preventing Clickjacking

MIME Type Confusion

Description
MIME type confusion can occur when a browser interprets files as a different type than intended, which could lead to security vulnerabilities like cross-site scripting (XSS).

Vulnerability found in /

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
X-Content-Type-Options is not set
                                    GET / HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/"
['OSHP-X-Content-Type-Options']
Solutions
Implement X-Content-Type-Options to prevent MIME type sniffing.
References
  • OWASP: MIME Sniffing
  • KeyCDN: Preventing MIME Type Sniffing

Unencrypted Channels

Description
Sensitive data must be protected when it is transmitted through the network.

Vulnerability found in /

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
No HTTPS redirection for this host. All HTTP requests are served in clear text.
                                    GET / HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0

curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/"
['WSTG-CRYP-03']

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/7c5afb

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
Sensitive data (GET parameters) was sent over an unencrypted HTTP connection to http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/7c5afb?panel=request. The server did not enforce HTTPS.
                                    GET /_profiler/7c5afb?panel=request HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br

curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/7c5afb?panel=request"
['WSTG-CRYP-03']

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/search

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
Sensitive data (cookie in the response) was sent over an unencrypted HTTP connection to http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request. The server redirected, but not to an HTTPS URL, leaving the initial data and the redirection exposed.
                                    GET /_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request"
['WSTG-CRYP-03']
Solutions
Use HTTPS for the whole web site and redirect any HTTP requests to HTTPS.
References
  • Testing for Sensitive Information Sent via Unencrypted Channels
  • Testing for Weak Transport Layer Security

Inconsistent Redirection

Description
An HTTP 3xx redirection response should typically contain only minimal content (or none), as clients are expected to follow the Location header. However, this response also contains HTML content (such as links or forms). This may confuse clients, expose unintended information, or allow attackers to craft malicious redirections.

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/search

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
3xx redirection contains unexpected HTML body (links/forms)
                                    GET /_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request"
['WSTG-INFO-05']

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/search

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
3xx redirection contains unexpected HTML body (links/forms)
                                    GET /_profiler/search HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search"
['WSTG-INFO-05']

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
3xx redirection contains unexpected HTML body (links/forms)
                                    GET /_profiler/ HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0

curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/"
['WSTG-INFO-05']

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/search

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
3xx redirection contains unexpected HTML body (links/forms)
                                    GET /_profiler/search?ip=default&status_code=1337&url=default&token=default&start=2023-03-03&end=2023-03-03&type=request&method= HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?ip=default&status_code=1337&url=default&token=default&start=2023-03-03&end=2023-03-03&type=request&method=" -e "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/7c5afb/search/results"
['WSTG-INFO-05']
Solutions
Ensure that 3xx HTTP responses only return the appropriate redirection headers and do not include unnecessary HTML content. If user feedback is required, provide a clear message without interactive elements (like links or forms). Always rely on the Location header for redirection logic.
References
  • ZAP Alert 10044-1: Inconsistent Redirection
  • MDN: HTTP Redirections
  • WSTG: Review Webpage Content for Information Leakage

Information Disclosure - Full Path

Description
The application response discloses full system paths. This information can help attackers understand the server environment, directory structure, and operating system, which can facilitate further attacks.

['WSTG-ERRH-01']
Solutions
Ensure that error messages and application responses do not disclose full filesystem paths or other sensitive system information. Use generic error messages for end users and log detailed errors only on the server side.
References
  • OWASP: Information Leakage
  • CWE-209: Generation of Error Message Containing Sensitive Information
  • WASC-13: Information Leakage

Secure Flag cookie

Description
The secure flag is an option that can be set by the application server when sending a new cookie to the user within an HTTP Response. The purpose of the secure flag is to prevent cookies from being observed by unauthorized parties due to the transmission of a the cookie in clear text.

Vulnerability found in /_profiler/search

Description HTTP Request cURL command line WSTG Code 
Secure flag is not set on the cookie: 'PHPSESSID' set at 'http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request'
                                    GET /_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request HTTP/1.1
                                    

                                    host: 127.0.0.1:8000
                                    

                                    connection: keep-alive
                                    

                                    user-agent: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.1; rv:45.0) Gecko/20100101 Firefox/45.0
                                    

                                    accept-language: en-US
                                    

                                    accept-encoding: gzip, deflate, br
                                    

                                    accept: text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8
                                    

                            
curl "http://127.0.0.1:8000/_profiler/search?limit=10&type=request"
['WSTG-SESS-02']
Solutions
When generating the cookie, make sure to set the Secure Flag to True.
References
  • OWASP: Testing for Cookies Attributes
  • OWASP: Secure Cookie Attribute

Internal Server Error

Description
An error occurred on the server's side, preventing it to process the request. It may be the sign of a vulnerability.
